SELECT c0.department_id AS "DepartmentId", d.department_name AS "DepartmentName", count(*)::int AS "Count"
FROM complaints AS c
INNER JOIN categories AS c0 ON c.category_id = c0.category_id
INNER JOIN departments AS d ON c0.department_id = d.department_id
WHERE c0.department_id = @departmentId
GROUP BY c0.department_id, d.department_name
ORDER BY count(*)::int DESC

INNER JOIN categories AS c0 ON c.category_id = c0.category_id
INNER JOIN priorities AS p ON c.priority_id = p.priority_id
LEFT JOIN employees AS e ON c.current_handler_employee_id = e.employee_id
WHERE c.escalation_due_at <= now() AND c.status_id <> 6 AND c.status_id <> 7 AND c.status_id <> 9 AND c.status_id <> 5

SELECT count(*)::int
FROM complaints AS c
INNER JOIN categories AS c0 ON c.category_id = c0.category_id
INNER JOIN complaint_statuses AS c1 ON c.status_id = c1.status_id
WHERE c0.department_id = @departmentId AND c.escalation_due_at IS NOT NULL AND ((c.resolved_at IS NULL AND NOT (c1.is_terminal) AND c.escalation_due_at < now()) OR (c.resolved_at IS NOT NULL AND c.status_id IN (5, 6) AND c.resolved_at > c.escalation_due_at))

SELECT c.category_id AS "CategoryId", c0.category_name AS "CategoryName", count(*)::int AS "Count"
FROM complaints AS c
INNER JOIN categories AS c0 ON c.category_id = c0.category_id
WHERE c0.department_id = @departmentId
GROUP BY c.category_id, c0.category_name
ORDER BY count(*)::int DESC

SELECT c0.department_id AS "DepartmentId", d.department_name AS "DepartmentName", count(*)::int AS "Count"
FROM complaints AS c
INNER JOIN categories AS c0 ON c.category_id = c0.category_id
INNER JOIN departments AS d ON c0.department_id = d.department_id
WHERE c0.department_id = @departmentId
GROUP BY c0.department_id, d.department_name
ORDER BY count(*)::int DESC

SELECT c.priority_id AS "PriorityId", p.priority_name AS "PriorityName", count(*)::int AS "Count"
FROM complaints AS c
INNER JOIN categories AS c0 ON c.category_id = c0.category_id
INNER JOIN priorities AS p ON c.priority_id = p.priority_id
WHERE c0.department_id = @departmentId
GROUP BY c.priority_id, p.priority_name
ORDER BY count(*)::int DESC
